      headers = {\n            \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36\'\n        }\n        \n Find search result links\n        results = []\n        result_links = soup.find_all(\'a\', class_=\'result__a\')\n        \n        for link in result_links[:max_results]:\n            title = link.get_text(strip=True)\n            url = link.get(\'href\', \'\')\n            \n            # Get snippet from nearby elements\n            snippet = \'\'\n            result_div = link.find_parent(\'div\', class_=\'result\')\n            if result_div:\n                snippet_elem = result_div.find(\'a\', class_=\'result__snippet\')\n                if snippet_elem:\n                    snippet = snippet_elem.get_text(strip=True)\n            \n            if title and url:\n                # Calculate relevance score for GameGrumps Mario Kart content\n                relevance = calculate_gamegrumps_relevance(title, snippet, url, query)\n                \n                results.append({\n                    \'title\': title,\n                    \'url\': url,\n url, query):\n    """Calculate relevance score specifically for GameGrumps Mario Kart content"""\n    text = (title + \' \' + snippet + \' \' + url).lower()\n    \n    score = 0\n    \n    # Essential terms (high weight)\n    essential_terms = {\n        \'gamegrumps\': 0.25,\n        \'game grumps\': 0.25,\n        \'mario kart 8 deluxe\': 0.3,\n        \'mario kart 8\': 0.25,\n        \'mk8d\': 0.2,\n        \'mk8\': 0.15\n    }\n    \n    for term, weight in essential_terms.items():\n        if term in text:\n            score += weight\n    \n    # Date-related terms (high weight for our specific search)\n    date_terms = {\n        \'may 2017\': 0.2,\n        \'2017\': 0.1,\n        \'may 14\': 0.25,\n        \'2017-05-14\': 0.3\n    }\n    \n    for term, weight in date_terms.items():\n        if term in text:\n            score += weight\n    \n    # YouTube bonus\n    if \'youtube.com\' in text or \'youtu.be\' in text:\n        score += 0.15\n    \n    # Nintendo Switch context (MK8D was a Switch launch title)\n    if \'nintendo switch\' in text or \'switch\' in text:\n        score += 0.1\n    \n    # Episode/series indicators\n    episode_terms = [\'episode\', \'part\', \'ep\', \'series\']\n    for term in episode_terms:\n        if term in text:\n            score += 0.05\n            break\n    \n    return min(score, 1.0)  # Cap at 1.0\n\nprint("Performing targeted searches...\\n")\n\nall_results = []\nfor query in search_queries:\n    results = search_duckduckgo(query, max_results=8)\n    all_results.extend(results)\n    time.sleep(2)  # Be respectful to search engine\n\nprint(f"\\nTotal search results collected: {len(all_results)}")\n\n# Remove duplicates based on URL\nseen_urls = set()\nunique_results = []\nfor parsing"""\n    print(f"  Searching DuckDuckGo for: \'{query}\'")\n    \n    try:\n        # CORRECTED: Use proper DuckDuckGo search URL\n        search_url = f"https://duckduckgo.com/html/?q={urllib.parse.quote(query)}"\n        \n        headers = {\n            \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like       for selector in result_selectors:\n            links = soup.select(selector)\n            if links:\n                result_links = links\n                print(f"    Found {len(links)} results using selector: {selector}")\n                break\n        \n        if not result_links:\n            # Fallback: find all links and filter for relevant ones\n            all_links = \'\'))]\n            print(f"    Fallback: Found {len(result_links)} YouTube links")\n        \n        for link in result_links[:max_results]:\n            title = link.get_text(strip=True)\n DuckDuckGo redirect\n                try:\n                    url = urllib.parse.unquote(url.split(\'uddg=\')[1])\n                except:\n                    pass\n            \n            # Get snippet from nearby elements\n            snippet = \'\'\n            parent = link.find_parent()\n            if parent:\n                # Look for description text near the link\n         if title and url and len(title) > 5:\n                # Calculate relevance score\n                relevance = calculate_gamegrumps_relevance(title, snippet, url, query)\n                \n content"""\n    text = (title + \' \' + snippet + \' \' + url).lower()\n    \n    score = 0\n    \n    # Essential terms (high weight)\n    if \'gamegrumps\' in text or \'game grumps\' in text:\n        score += 0.3\n    \n    if \'mario kart 8 deluxe\' in text:\n        score += 0.25\n    elif \'mario kart 8\' in text:\n        score += 0.2\n    elif \'mario kart\' in text:\n        score += 0.15\n    \n    # Date-related terms\n    if \'may 2017\' in text:\n        score += 0.2\n    elif \'2017\' in text:\n        score += 0.1\n    \n    if \'may 14\' in text or \'2017-05-14\' in text:\n or \'switch\' in text:\n        score += 0.05\n    \n    return min(score, 1.0)\n\nprint("Performing corrected searches...\\n")\n\nall_results = []\nfor i, query in enumerate(search_queries, 1):\n Use yt-dlp to get channel video list with much longer timeout\n        cmd = [\n            \'yt-dlp\',\n            \'--dump-json\',\n            \'--playlist-end\', str(max_videos),\n            \'--no-download\',\n            \'--socket-timeout\', \'180\',  # 3 minutes socket timeout\n            channel_url\n        ]\n        \n        print(f"    Executing with extended timeout (180s): yt-dlp --dump-json --playlist-end {max_videos} [channel]")\n        print(f"    This may take several minutes...")\n        \n        # Extended timeout of 300 seconds (5 minutes)\n        result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=300)\n        \n        if result.returncode != 0:\n            print(f"    Error accessing channel: {result.stderr[:300]}...")\n            return []\n        \n        # Parse the JSON output\n        videos = []\n        for line in result.stdout.strip().split(\'\\n\'):\n            if line.strip():\n                try:\n                    video_info = json.loads(line)\n                    videos.append(video_info)\n                except json.JSONDecodeError:\n                    continue\n        \n        print(f"    Successfully retrieved {len(videos)} videos from channel")\n        return videos\n        \n    except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:\n        print(f"    Channel access timed out after 300 seconds")\n        return []\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f"    Error: {e}")\n        return []\n\nprint("Attempting to access GameGrumps channel with extended timeout...\\n")\nchannel_videos = get_channel_videos_with_extended_timeout(gamegrumps_channel_url, max_videos=100)\n\nif not channel_videos:\n    print("Channel access failed. 4 minutes\n                f\'ytsearch{max_results}:{query}\'\n            ]\n            \n            # 6 minute timeout\n            result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=360)\n            \n            if result.returncode != 0:\n                print(f"      Search failed: {result.stderr[:200]}...")\n                return []\n            \n            videos = []\n            for line in result.stdout.strip().split(\'\\n\'):\n                if line.strip():\n                    try:\n                        video_info = json.loads(line)\n                        videos.append(video_info)\n                    except json.JSONDecodeError:\n                        continue\n            \n            print(f"      Found {len(videos)} videos")\n            return videos\n            \n        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:\n            print(f"      Search timed out after 360 seconds")\n            return []\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f"      Error: {e}")\n            return []\n    \n    all_videos = []\n    for query in launch_period_queries:\n        videos = search_with_extended_timeout(query, max_results=8)\n        all_videos.extend(videos)\n        if videos:  # If we got some results, continue\n            time.sleep(3)\n        else:\n            print(f"      No results for this query, trying next...")\n    \n    channel_videos = all_videos\n\nprint(f"\\nTotal videos retrieved: {len(channel_videos)}")\n\nif not channel_videos:\n    print("\\n=== STEP 4: FALLBACK - MANUAL VIDEO IDENTIFICATION ===\\n")\n    print("All automated searches failed. Implementing manual approach...")\n    \n    # Based on research, let\'s try some known GameGrumps video patterns\n    # GameGrumps typically uploads daily, so May 14, 2017 would have specific videos\n    \n    # Check if it\'s GameGrumps content\n        is_gamegrumps = \'game grumps\' in uploader or \'gamegrumps\' in uploader\n        \n        # Check for May 2017\n        is_may_2017 = upload_date.startswith(\'2017-05\') if upload_date else False\n        \n        if is_may_2017:\n            may_2017_videos.append(video)\n            print(f"  May 2017 video: {video.get(\'title\', \'Unknown\')[:50]}... ({upload_date})")\n        \n        # Check for Mario Kart content\n        mk_score = 0\n        evidence = []\n        \n        if \'mario kart 8 deluxe\' in title:\n            mk_score += 5\n            evidence.append(\'Title: Mario Kart 8 Deluxe\')\n        elif \'mario kart 8\' in title:\n            mk_score += 4\n            evidence.append(\'Title: Mario Kart 8\')\n        elif \'mario kart\' in title:\n            mk_score += 3\n            evidence.append(\'Title: Mario Kart\')\n        \n        if \'mario kart\' in description:\n            mk_score += 1\n            evidence.append(\'Description: Mario Kart\')\n        \n        if \'deluxe\' in title or \'deluxe\' in description:\n            mk_score += 2\n            evidence.append(\'Deluxe mentioned\')\n        \n        if \'switch\' in title or \'nintendo switch\' in description:\n            mk_score += 1\n            evidence.append(\'Nintendo Switch\')\n        \n        if mk_score > 0 and is_gamegrumps:\n            candidate_info = {\n                \'title\': video.get(\'title\', \'\'),\n                \'url\': video.get(\'webpage_url\', \'\'),\n                \'upload_date\': upload_date,\n                \'duration\': video.get(\'duration\', 0),\n                \'uploader\': video.get(\'uploader\', \'\'),\n                \'mk_score\': mk_score,\n                \'evidence\': evidence,\n                \'is_may_2017\': is_may_2017,\n                \'is_target_date\': upload_date == target_date,\n                \'view_count\': video.get(\'view_count\', 0)\n            }\n            mario_kart_candidates.append(candidate_info)\n    \n    # {title}")\n                            \n                            if start_time <= 120 < chapter.get(\'end_time\', float(\'inf\')):\n                                print(f"    *** 2-minute mark is in: {title} ***")\n                    \n                    # Save detailed info\n                    detail_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'target_video_analysis.json\')\n                    with open(detail_file, \'w\') as f:\n                        json.dump(detailed_info, f, indent=2)\n                    print(f"\\nDetailed video info saved to: {os.path.basename(detail_file)}")\n                    \n            except Exception as e:\n                print(f"Could not get detailed video info: {e}")\n        \n        else:\n            print(f"Best candidate is too short ({best_candidate[\'duration\']} seconds) for 2-minute analysis")\n    \n    else:\n        print(f"\\nNo Mario Kart candidates found in the retrieved videos.")\n    \n    search_results[\'video_candidates\'] = mario_kart_candidates\n\nelse:\n    print(f"\\nNo videos could be retrieved from any method.")\n    print(f"\\nFinal recommendation: Manual search approach")\n    print(f"1. Check the 2-minute timestamp for the racetrack")\n\nprint(f"\\n=== STEP 7: FINAL RESULTS AND SUMMARY ===\\n")\n\n# Create comprehensive analysis\nanalysis_summary = {\n    \'search_methods_attempted\': [\n        \'Direct channel access with extended timeout\',\n        \'Extended timeout search queries\',\n        \'Specific video URL analysis\'\n    ],\n    \'total_videos_analyzed\': len(channel_videos),\n    \'mario_kart_candidates\': len(mario_kart_candidates) if \'mario_kart_candidates\' in locals() else 0,\n    \'target_video_found\': len(mario_kart_candidates) > 0 if \'mario_kart_candidates\' in locals() else False,\n    \'search_effectiveness\': \'High\' if \'mario_kart_candidates\' in locals() and mario_kart_candidates else \'Low\'\n}\n\nsearch_results[\'analysis_summary\'] = analysis_summary\n\nprint(f"Final Analysis Summary:")\nprint(f"  Methods attempted: {len(analysis_summary[\'search_methods_attempted\'])}")\nprint(f"  Videos analyzed: {analysis_summary[\'total_videos_analyzed\']}")\nprint(f"  Mario Kart candidates: {analysis_summary[\'mario_kart_candidates\']}")\nprint(f"  Target video found: {analysis_summary[\'target_video_found\']}")\nprint(f"  Overall effectiveness: {analysis_summary[\'search_effectiveness\']}")\n\n# Save results\nresults_file = os.path.join(workspace_dir, \'extended_timeout_search_results.json\')\nwith open(results_file, \'w\') as f:\n    json.dump(search_results, f, indent=2)\n\nprint(f"\\nSearch results saved to: {os.path.basename(results_file)}")\n\n# Create final report\nfinal_report = f"""GAMEGRUMPS MARIO KART 8 DELUXE SEARCH - EXTENDED TIMEOUT APPROACH\n===================================================================\n\nOBJECTIVE:\nFind GameGrumps YouTube video from May 14, 2017 featuring Mario Kart 8 Deluxe.\nIdentify racetrack at 2-minute timestamp.\n\nMETHODS ATTEMPTED:\n1.     "code": 'import os\nimport subprocess\nimport json\nfrom datetime import datetime\nimport time\n\nprint("=== GAMEGRUMPS MARIO KART 8 DELUXE - TARGETED VIDEO SEARCH ===\\n")\nprint("Objective: Find GameGrumps YouTube video from May 14, 2017 featuring Mario Kart 8 Deluxe")\nprint("Target: Identify racetrack at 2-minute timestamp\\n")\n\n# Create workspace directory\nworkspace_dir = "workspace"\nos.makedirs(workspace_dir, exist_ok=True)\n\nprint("=== STEP 1: DIRECT YOUTUBE SEARCH WITH SPECIFIC DATE CONSTRAINTS ===\\n")\n\n# Based on the previous analysis, let\'s try a more targeted approach\n# GameGrumps Mario Kart 8 Deluxe was likely uploaded shortly after the game\'s release (April 28, 2017)\n\ndef search_youtube_with_date_filter(query, upload_date=None):\n    """Search YouTube using yt-dlp with date filtering"""\n    print(f"  Searching YouTube: \'{query}\'")\n    if upload_date:\n        print(f"  Date filter: {upload_date}")\n    \n    try:\n        # Construct yt-dlp command with date filtering\n        cmd = [\n            \'yt-dlp\',\n            \'--dump-json\',\n            \'--no-download\',\n            \'--playlist-end\', \'20\',\n            f\'ytsearch20:{query}\'\n        ]\n        \n        print(f"    Executing search with 180s timeout...")\n        result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=180)\n        \n        if result.returncode != 0:\n            print(f"    Search failed: {result.stderr[:300]}...")\n            return []\n        \n        # Parse results\n        videos = []\n        for line in result.stdout.strip().split(\'\\n\'):\n            if line.strip():\n                try:\n                    video_info = json.loads(line)\n                    videos.append(video_info)\n                except json.JSONDecodeError:\n                    continue\n        \n        print(f"    Found {len(videos)} videos")\n        return videos\n        \n    except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:\n        print(f"    Search timed out after 180 seconds")\n        return []\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f"    Error: {e}")\n        return []\n\n# Try very specific search queries\ntargeted_queries = [\n    \'GameGrumps "Mario Kart 8 Deluxe" May 2017\',\n    \'Game Grumps Mario Kart 8 Deluxe 2017-05-14\',\n    \'GameGrumps Mario Kart 8 Deluxe Nintendo Switch May\',\n    \'Arin Dan Mario Kart 8 Deluxe GameGrumps\'\n]\n\nall_videos = []\nfor query in targeted_queries:\n    videos = search_youtube_with_date_filter(query)\n    if videos:\n        all_videos.extend(videos)\n        print(f"  Added {len(videos)} videos\\n")\n        time.sleep(3)  # Rate limiting\n    else:\n        print(f"  No results, trying next query\\n")\n        time.sleep(1)\n\nprint(f"Total videos collected: {len(all_videos)}")\n\nprint("\\n=== STEP 2: FILTERING AND ANALYZING CANDIDATES ===\\n")\n\n# Filter for GameGrumps content from May 2017\ntarget_date = \'2017-05-14\'\nmay_2017_candidates = []\ngamegrumps_candidates = []\n\nfor video in all_videos:\n    title = video.get(\'title\', \'\')\n    uploader = video.get(\'uploader\', \'\').lower()\n    channel = video.get(\'channel\', \'\').lower()\n    upload_date = video.get(\'upload_date\', \'\')\n    duration = video.get(\'duration\', 0)\n    url = video.get(\'webpage_url\', \'\')\n    \n    # Check if it\'s GameGrumps\n    is_gamegrumps = any(term in uploader for term in [\'game grumps\', \'gamegrumps\']) or \\\n                   any(term in channel for term in [\'game grumps\', \'gamegrumps\'])\n    \n    if is_gamegrumps:\n        gamegrumps_candidates.append(video)\n        print(f"  GameGrumps video: {title[:50]}... ({upload_date})")\n        \n        # Check for Mario Kart 8 Deluxe content\n        title_lower = title.lower()\n        mk8d_score = 0\n        evidence = []\n        \n        if \'mario kart 8 deluxe\' in title_lower:\n            mk8d_score += 5\n            evidence.append(\'Mario Kart 8 Deluxe in title\')\n        elif \'mario kart 8\' in title_lower:\n            mk8d_score += 4\n            evidence.append(\'Mario Kart 8 in title\')\n        elif \'mario kart\' in title_lower:\n            mk8d_score += 3\n            evidence.append(\'Mario Kart in title\')\n        \n        if \'deluxe\' in title_lower:\n            mk8d_score += 2\n            evidence.append(\'Deluxe mentioned\')\n        \n        # Date scoring\n        is_may_2017 = upload_date.startswith(\'2017-05\') if upload_date else False\n        is_target_date = upload_date == target_date if upload_date else False\n        \n        if is_target_date:\n            mk8d_score += 10\n            evidence.append(\'Exact target date match\')\n        elif is_may_2017:\n            mk8d_score += 5\n            evidence.append(\'May 2017 upload\')\n        \n        if mk8d_score > 0 and duration >= 120:  # At least 2 minutes\n            candidate_info = {\n                \'title\': title,\n                \'url\': url,\n                \'upload_date\': upload_date,\n                \'duration\': duration,\n                \'uploader\': video.get(\'uploader\', \'\'),\n                \'mk8d_score\': mk8d_score,\n                \'evidence\': evidence,\n                \'is_target_date\': is_target_date,\n                \'is_may_2017\': is_may_2017,\n                \'view_count\': video.get(\'view_count\', 0)\n            }\n            may_2017_candidates.append(candidate_info)\n\nprint(f"\\nFiltering results:")\nprint(f"  GameGrumps videos: {len(gamegrumps_candidates)}")\nprint(f"  Mario Kart candidates (2+ min): {len(may_2017_candidates)}")\n\n# Sort by score\nmay_2017_candidates.sort(key=lambda x: x[\'mk8d_score\'], reverse=True)\n\nprint("\\n=== STEP 3: ANALYZING TOP CANDIDATES ===\\n")\n\nif may_2017_candidates:\n    print("Top Mario Kart 8 Deluxe candidates:")\n    \n    for i, candidate in enumerate(may_2017_candidates[:3], 1):\n        print(f"\\n{i}. {candidate[\'title\']}")\n        print(f"   URL: {candidate[\'url\']}")\n        print(f"   Upload Date: {candidate[\'upload_date\']}")\n        print(f"   Duration: {candidate[\'duration\']//60}:{candidate[\'duration\']%60:02d}")\n        print(f"   Score: {candidate[\'mk8d_score\']}")\n        print(f"   Evidence: {\', \'.join(candidate[\'evidence\'])}")\n        print(f"   Target Date: {\'Yes\' if candidate[\'is_target_date\'] else \'No\'}")\n        print(f"   Views: {candidate[\'view_count\']:,}")\n    \n    # Analyze the best candidate\n    best_candidate = may_2017_candidates[0]\n    \n    print(f"\\n=== STEP 4: DETAILED ANALYSIS OF BEST CANDIDATE ===\\n")\n    print(f"*** BEST CANDIDATE IDENTIFIED ***")\n    print(f"Title: {best_candidate[\'title\']}")\n    print(f"URL: {best_candidate[\'url\']}")\n    print(f"Upload Date: {best_candidate[\'upload_date\']}")\n    print(f"Duration: {best_candidate[\'duration\']//60}:{best_candidate[\'duration\']%60:02d}")\n    print(f"Score: {best_candidate[\'mk8d_score\']}")\n    \n    # Get detailed video information\n    print(f"\\nGetting detailed video information...")\n    \n    try:\n        cmd = [\'yt-dlp\', \'--dump-json\', \'--no-download\', best_candidate[\'url\']]\n        result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=60)\n        \n        if result.returncode == 0:\n            detailed_info = json.loads(result.stdout)\n            \n            # Look for chapters\n            chapters = detailed_info.get(\'chapters\', [])\n            if chapters:\n                print(f"\\nVideo chapters found:")\n                for chapter in chapters:\n                    start_time = chapter.get(\'start_time\', 0)\n                    end_time = chapter.get(\'end_time\', 0)\n                    title = chapter.get(\'title\', \'Unknown\')\n                    print(f"  {start_time//60}:{start_time%60:02d} - {end_time//60}:{end_time%60:02d}: {title}")\n                    \n                    if start_time <= 120 <= end_time:\n                        print(f"    *** 2-minute mark is in this chapter: {title} ***")\n            \n            # Save detailed info\n  }\n}\n\nprint("Mario Kart 8 Deluxe Speedrunning Categories:")\nfor category, details in mk8dx_categories.items():\n    print(f"\\n{category.replace(\'_\', \' \').title()}:")\n    print(f"   Position: {stadium_info[\'position\']}")\n        print(f"    Typical Record Range: {stadium_info[\'typical_record_range\']}")\n\nprint("\\n=== STEP 3: ACCESSING WORLD RECORD DATABASES ===\\n")\n\ndef search_world_records(source_info):\n    """Search for Mario Kart 8 Deluxe world records"""\n    print(f"--- Accessing {source_info[\'name\']} ---")\n    print(f"URL: {source_info[\'url\']}")\n    \n    try:\n        headers = {\n            \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 filename = f"{source_info[\'name\'].replace(\' \', \'_\').lower()}.html"\n            filepath = os.path.join(workspace_dir, filename)\n            \n            with open(filepath, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                f.write(response.text)\n            \n            print(f"Content saved to: {filename}")\n            \n            # Parse for Mario Kart Stadium records\n            soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, \'html.parser\')\n            \n            # Look for Mario Kart Stadium mentions\n            stadium_mentions = []\n            text_content = soup.get_text().lower()\n            \n            if \'mario kart stadium\' in text_content:\n                print(f"Found \'Mario Kart Stadium\' mentions in content")\n                \n                # Extract relevant sections\n                lines = text_content.split(\'\\n\')\n                for i, line in enumerate(lines):\n                    if \'mario kart stadium\' in line.lower():\n                        # Get context around the mention\n                        context_start = max(0, i-2)\n                        context_end = min(len(lines), i+3)\n                        context = lines[context_start:context_end]\n                        stadium_mentions.append({\n                            \'line_number\': i,\n                            \'content\': line.strip(),\n                            \'context\': context\n                        })\n            \n            # Look for time patterns (1:XX.XXX format)\n            import re\n            time_pattern = r\'\\b1:[0-5][0-9]\\.[0-9]{3}\\b\'\n            time_matches = re.findall(time_pattern, response.text)\n            \n            if time_matches:\n                print(f"Found {len(time_matches)} potential time records: {time_matches[:5]}...")\n            \n            return {\n                \'success\': True,\n                \'content_length\': len(response.text),\n                \'stadium_mentions\': len(stadium_mentions),\n                \'time_matches\': time_matches[:10],  # First 10 matches\n                \'filename\': filename\n            }\n        else:\n            print(f"Failed to access (Status: {response.status_code})")\n            return {\'success\': False, \'status_code\': response.status_code}\n            \n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f"Error accessing {source_info[\'name\']}: {e}")\n        return {\'success\': False, \'error\': str(e)}\n\n# Search each source\nsearch_results = []\nfor source in world_record_sources:\n    result = search_world_records(source)\n    result[\'source\'] = source[\'name\']\n    search_results.append(result)\n    print()\n    time.sleep(2)  # Rate limiting\n\nprint("=== STEP 4: ANALYZING sources:")\n\nfor result in successful_sources:\n    print(f"\\n{result[\'source\']}:")\n    print(f"  Content length: {result[\'content_length\']:,} characters")\n    print(f"  Stadium mentions: {result[\'stadium_mentions\']}")\n    print(f"  Time matches found: {len(result.get(\'time_matches\', []))}")\n    if result.get(\'time_matches\'):\n        print(f"  Sample times: {result[\'time_matches\'][:3]}")\n\nprint("\\n=== STEP 5: DETAILED ANALYSIS OF SUCCESSFUL SOURCES ===\\n")\n\n# Analyze the content of successful sources for Mario Kart Stadium records\n                    context_lines = lines[max(0, i-3):min(len(lines), i+4)]\n                    \n                    for context_line in context_lines:\n                        # Look for time patterns\n                        import re\n                        time_patterns = [\n                            r\'\\b1:[0-5][0-9]\\.[0-9]{3}\\b\',  # 1:XX.XXX\n                            r\'\\b1:[0-5][0-9]\\.[0-9]{2}\\b\',   # 1:XX.XX\n                            r\'\\b[0-5][0-9]\\.[0-9]{3}\\b\'     # XX.XXX (seconds only)\n                        ]\n                        \n                        for pattern in time_patterns:\n                            matches = re.findall(pattern, context_line)\n                            if matches:\n                                record_info = {\n                                    \'source\': result[\'source\'],\n                                    \'track\': \'Mario Kart Stadium\',\n                                    \'times\': matches,\n                                    \'context\': line.strip(),\n                                    \'full_context\': [cl.strip() for cl in context_lines if cl.strip()]\n                                }\n                                stadium_records.append(record_info)\n                                print(f"  Found potential record: {matches} in context of \'{line.strip()[:100]}...\'")\n                                break\n        \n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f"Error analyzing {result[\'source\']}: {e}")\n\nprint(f"\\nTotal           # Look for Mario Kart Stadium mentions\n                stadium_keywords = [\'mario kart stadium\', \'stadium\', \'mks\', \'mushroom cup\']\n                stadium_mentions = 0\n                \n                for keyword in stadium_keywords:\n                    stadium_mentions += text_content.count(keyword)\n                \n                # Look for time patterns\n all_times = []\n            for pattern in time_patterns:\n                matches = re.findall(pattern, response.text)\n                all_times.extend(matches)\n            \n            # Filter for likely Mario Kart Stadium times (1:30-1:40 range)\n            stadium_candidate_times = []\n            for time_str in all_times:\n                if time_str.startswith(\'1:3\'):\n print(f"Total time patterns: {len(all_times)}")\n            print(f"Stadium time candidates: {len(stadium_candidate_times)}")\n            \n            if stadium_candidate_times:\n \'stadium_mentions\': stadium_mentions,\n                \'record_mentions\': record_mentions,\n                \'all_times\': all_times[:20],\n                \'stadium_times\': characters")\n    print(f"  Stadium mentions: {result[\'stadium_mentions\']}")\n    print(f"  Record mentions: {result[\'record_mentions\']}")\n    print(f"  Stadium time candidates: 100:  # 1:30 - 1:40 range\n                                    record_finding = {\n                                        \'source\': result[\'source\'],\n
